              | (df["AROOND_14_4h"] < 70.0)
            )
            # 15m & 1h up move, 15m & 1h & 4h still high, 1h & 4h downtrend, 15m still high, 4h high & overbought
            & (
              (df["RSI_3_15m"] < 65.0)
              | (df["RSI_3_1h"] < 40.0)
              | (df["RSI_14_15m"] > 60.0)
              | (df["RSI_14_1h"] > 50.0)

              | (df["AROOND_14_15m"] < 40.0)
              | (df["AROOND_14_4h"] < 70.0)
              | (df["ROC_9_4h"] > -10.0)

              | (df["STOCHRSIk_14_14_3_3_4h"] > 60.0)
              | (df["ROC_9_1d"] > -50.0)
            )

            & (df["close"] < (df["close_min_12"] * 0.65))

          short_entry_logic.append(
            (df["RSI_20"] < df["RSI_20"].shift(1))
            & (df["RSI_4"] > 55.0)
            & (df["RSI_14"] < 68.0)

            & (df["close"] < df["SMA_16"] * 0.965)
            & (df["close"] < df["SMA_16_1h"] * 0.985)
          )

        if short_entry_condition_index == 904:
